############################################################################################################################
# 
# Adaptations of events from the CK2 version of VIET Events
# VIETold.2000-VIETold.2999 reserved for events made towards the end of CK2's life cycle
# Fired from the on_actions for every one, two, five, and ten years depending on rarity
# 
# 
# ##### GRAND LIST OF EVENTS #####
# 
# 2001-2012		Oblivion Soundtrack Inspired
# 2013-2018		Reading Stories
# 2019-2026		Stuck Inside
# 2027-2040		Fantastical Stories
# 2041-2053		Prophecy and Future
# 2054-2067		Skyrim Dialogue Inspired
# 2068-2073		Sun
# 2074-2093		Generic (was inspired by CK2 event pics when made)
# 2094-2128		Death
# 2129-2150		Generic (part of the first batch of events made for CK2 VIET Events Reborn)
# 2151-2161		Generic 2 (part of the first batch of events made for CK2 VIET Events Reborn)
# 2162-2170		Medicine
# 2171-2173		Broccoli
# 2174-2188		Strange Dreams
# 2189-2210		Spices and Herbs (A-L mostly)
# 2211-2213		Rosewater
# 2214-2224		Oblivion Inspired
# 2225-2231		Rose
# 2232-2233		Childhood Generic
# 2234-2236		Generic for 3rd anniversary
# 2237-2244		Night
# 2245-2250 	Swansong 2 (Final events made for VIET Events Reborn)
# 
############################################################################################################################

namespace = VIETold


##################################################
# OBLIVION SOUNDTRACK INSPIRED	2001-2012
##################################################

# Through the Valleys - Dream of Lake Rumare
VIETold.2001 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2001.t
	desc = VIETold.2001.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_oblivion_pastoral_dream
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_content
	}	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Go to Lake Rumare
		name = VIETold.2001.a	
		stress_impact = {
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lake_rumare_dream_lake
			days = 1095
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Go to the Wayshrine
		name = VIETold.2001.b
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lake_rumare_dream_wayshrine
			days = 1095
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Go to the forest
		name = VIETold.2001.c
		stress_impact = {
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lake_rumare_dream_forest
			days = 1095
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Go to the cottage
		name = VIETold.2001.d
		stress_impact = {
			gluttonous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lake_rumare_dream_cottage
			days = 1095
		}		
	}
}

# Harvest Dawn - passing by peasants doing farm work
VIETold.2002 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2002.t
	desc = VIETold.2002.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_tuscan_country
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_honorable
	}	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Carry on
		name = VIETold.2002.a	
		VIET_random_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}	
	option = { # Lower class scum!
		name = VIETold.2002.b	
		add_dread = 5
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Talk to commoners
		name = VIETold.2002.c
		VIET_random_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# King and Country - existential crisis about purpose as a ruler
VIETold.2003 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2003.t
	desc = VIETold.2003.desc
	theme = stewardship_duty_focus
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Do what's important in life
		name = VIETold.2003.a
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Do great deeds
		name = VIETold.2003.b
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Happiness is what matters most
		name = VIETold.2003.c
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Why even try
		name = VIETold.2003.d
		add_dread = 4
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}		
	}
}

# All's Well - nothing exciting happened in court today

	desc = VIETold.2005.desc
	theme = vassal
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = boredom
	}	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Type B Personality
		name = VIETold.2005.a
		custom_tooltip = VIETold.2005.a.tooltip
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Type A Personality
		name = VIETold.2005.b
		custom_tooltip = VIETold.2005.b.tooltip
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}



# Watchman's Ease - talking with guard on duty
VIETold.2006 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2006.t
	desc = VIETold.2006.desc
	theme = friendly	
	override_background = { reference = corridor_day }
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Continue
		name = VIETold.2006.a
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}	
	option = { # Stand up straight!
		name = VIETold.2006.b
		random_list = {
			30 = { }
			30 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { add_dread = 5 }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Be more vigilant!
		name = VIETold.2006.c
		random_list = {
			30 = { }
			10 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			30 = { add_dread = 5 }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Glory of Cyrodiil - what is my purpose as a ruler?
VIETold.2007 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2007.t
	desc = VIETold.2007.desc
	theme = family
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Unsure
		name = VIETold.2007.a
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_dread = 5 }
			10 = { VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Be an evil douche
		name = VIETold.2007.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				has_trait = just
				has_trait = generous
				has_trait = forgiving
			}
		}
		add_dread = 5
	}	
	option = { # Protect and help subjects
		name = VIETold.2007.c
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = callous
				has_trait = sadistic
			}
		}
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}
	option = { # Win glory
		name = VIETold.2007.d
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = humble
				has_trait = craven
			}
		}
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}
}

		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2

		}
	}
	
	option = { # I cry too

		name = VIETold.2008.b

			modifier = VIET_unmoved_by_art

		}
	}
}

# Auriel's Ascension - a deity manifests themselves (was a province event in old VIET)
VIETold.2009 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2009.t
	desc = VIETold.2009.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_ancient_cairn
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_zealous
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Nice
		name = VIETold.2009.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_auriels_ascension
			years = 5
		}
	}	
	option = { # It's a cult!
		name = VIETold.2009.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_repressing_auriels_ascension_cult
			years = 5
		}
	}	
	option = { # No opinion
		name = VIETold.2009.c
		# Because no good OR bad effects?
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}
}

# Peace of Akatosh - is peace a worthwhile ideal?
VIETold.2012 = {
	type = character_event

	desc = VIETold.2012.desc
	theme = realm
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_content
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	option = { # SMITE INFIDELS
		name = VIETold.2012.a
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Love and peace
		name = VIETold.2012.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						has_doctrine_parameter = pacifist_opinion_active 
						trait_is_virtue = calm					
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						has_doctrine = tenet_warmonger 
						trait_is_virtue = wrathful					
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_tiny_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}		
		stress_impact = {
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Silly rabbit, cynicism is for kids
		name = VIETold.2012.c
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}
}

	title = VIETold.2025.t
	desc = VIETold.2025.desc
	theme = unfriendly

	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = paranoia
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Huh
		name = VIETold.2025.a
		add_stress = 3
	}
}



# Staying up late at night a lot

	desc = VIETold.2026.desc
	theme = intrigue
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = boredom
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Oh dear
		name = VIETold.2026.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Try to make the most of it
		name = VIETold.2026.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_late_night_work
			days = 1111
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = medium_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Rumors about incestuous marriage in faraway lands
VIETold.2027 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2027.t
	desc = VIETold.2027.desc
	theme = learning
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}

	trigger = {
		faith = {
			NOR = {
				has_doctrine = tenet_divine_marriage
				has_doctrine = doctrine_consanguinity_unrestricted
			}		
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Barbaric
		name = VIETold.2027.a
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Open minded
		name = VIETold.2027.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_open_minded_about_incest
			days = 730
		}
		VIET_tiny_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Horny
		name = VIETold.2027.c
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = chaste
				has_trait = celibate
				has_sexuality = asexual
			}
		}
		VIET_tiny_piety_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_tiny_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_deviant_opinion
			days = 730
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Skeptical
		name = VIETold.2027.d
		#trigger = {
		#	trait = cynical
		#}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_skeptical_about_fantasy_stories
			days = 730
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

	}

		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		# Less likely to happen within Egypt area, because event is about a traveler to Egypt
		modifier = {
			add = -0.4
			capital_province = {
				geographical_region = world_africa_north_east
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Amazing
		name = VIETold.2029.a

			days = 654
		}

			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}		
	option = { # Are they still around?
		name = VIETold.2029.c

		}

# Traveler tells of a golden island beyond Japan
VIETold.2030 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2030.t
	desc = VIETold.2030.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = admiration
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		# Shouldn't happen close to Japan
		capital_province = {
			NOR = {
				geographical_region = world_asia_japan
				geographical_region = world_asia_sakhalin_hokkaido
				geographical_region = world_asia_north_east
				geographical_region = world_asia_korea
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		# Less likely to happen outside of India, Central Asia, and the Middle East, as people didn't travel that far
		modifier = {
			add = -0.5
			capital_province = {
				NOR = {
					geographical_region = world_africa_north_east
					geographical_region = world_africa_east
					geographical_region = world_steppe
					geographical_region = world_middle_east
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_india
					geographical_region = world_burma
					geographical_region = world_tibet
					geographical_region = world_siberia
					geographical_region = world_asia
					#geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Amazing
		name = VIETold.2030.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_thinking_about_foreign_lands
			days = 700
		}
	}	
	option = { # O rly?
		name = VIETold.2030.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_skeptical_about_fantasy_stories
			days = 700
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Story of the labyrinth a la the Minotaur
VIETold.2032 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2032.t
	desc = VIETold.2032.desc
	theme = realm
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
	}
	
	option = { # They deserve freedom
		name = VIETold.2032.a
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_dread = -3
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # It is unnecessary
		name = VIETold.2032.b
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_dread = -3
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Sounds fun!
		name = VIETold.2032.c
		add_dread = 6
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

			has_trait = lustful
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Sounds nice
		name = VIETold.2033.a

			10 = { VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes }

		}

# Old man recounts meeting the Dreamer - will be large event chain later about a mysterious figure appearing in dreams, maybe ambiguous conicidence, maybe actual otherworldly figure
VIETold.2034 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2034.t
	desc = VIETold.2034.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Type A is bad
		name = VIETold.2034.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = calm					
						trait_is_virtue = content					
						trait_is_virtue = patient					
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = brave					
						trait_is_virtue = ambitious					
						trait_is_virtue = impatient					
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Type B is bad
		name = VIETold.2034.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = brave					
						trait_is_virtue = ambitious					
						trait_is_virtue = impatient					
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
			VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = calm					
						trait_is_virtue = content					
						trait_is_virtue = patient					
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
			VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # You met the Dreamer too?
		name = VIETold.2034.c
		trigger = {
			#has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer
			exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
		}
		# Add to a Dreamer variable???
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		change_variable = {
			name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

		}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2

		}
	}
	

	
	option = { # Curious!

		}

# Guard claims to have met a woman in white/lady in white (a common type of spirit in various folklores around the world)
VIETold.2036 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2036.t
	desc = VIETold.2036.desc
	theme = skull	
	override_background = { reference = corridor_day }
	
	left_portrait = root

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	

	
	option = { # What a coward lol
		name = VIETold.2036.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			days = 365
		}
		stress_impact = {
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2036.info
		}
	}	
	option = { # Frightening things beyond!
		name = VIETold.2036.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_heard_eerie_story
			days = 365
		}
		stress_impact = {
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2036.info
		}
	}
}

# Maid recounts meeting the Dreamer (female Dreamer; there is both a Male and Female Dreamer in the event chain, who are ambiguously connected)
VIETold.2037 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2037.t
	desc = VIETold.2037.desc
	theme = friendly	
	override_background = { reference = corridor_day }
	
	left_portrait = root

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	

	
	option = { # Very odd
		name = VIETold.2037.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_heard_eerie_story
			days = 365
		}
	}

		name = VIETold.2037.b
		trigger = {
			#has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer

		}
		# Add to a Dreamer variable???
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		change_variable = {
			name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2040.t
	desc = VIETold.2040.desc
	theme = realm
	
	left_portrait = root

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
	}
	

	
	option = { # It's made up
		name = VIETold.2040.a
		trigger = {
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		trait = cynical
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}	
	option = { # Pink skin
		name = VIETold.2040.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}	
	option = { # Dark blue skin
		name = VIETold.2040.c
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}	
	option = { # Green skin
		name = VIETold.2040.d
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			5 = { VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
	}	
	option = { # I don't know the answer, the truth I cannot infer.
		name = VIETold.2040.e
		random_list = {
			5 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
	}
}

# Prophetic dream of World War 1
VIETold.2041 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2041.t
	desc = VIETold.2041.desc
	theme = battle
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = fear
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_serious_events }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_had_WW1_dream }
		NOT = { has_global_variable = VIET_WW1_prophecy_happened }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_flag = VIET_had_WW1_dream
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2041.a		
		trigger_event = {
			id = VIETold.2042
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

# Witness the great war
VIETold.2043 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2043.t
	desc = VIETold.2043.desc
	theme = battle
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = shock
	}
	
	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = mx_cue_crusade_starts 
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2043.a	
		stress_impact = {
			base = medium_stress_impact_gain
			craven = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_world_war_1_dream
			#days = 1918
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = VIET_WW1_prophecy_happened
			value = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = callous
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = callous
				add_trait = compassionate
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = sadistic
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = sadistic
				add_trait = compassionate
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = trusting
				add_trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = vengeful
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = vengeful
				add_trait = forgiving
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = wrathful
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = wrathful
				add_trait = calm
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = arrogant
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = arrogant
				add_trait = humble
			}
		}
	}
}

# Seer predicts the coming of Genghis Khan
VIETold.2044 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2044.t
	desc = VIETold.2044.desc
	theme = crown
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_genghis_khan_prophecy }
		NOT = { has_global_variable = mongols_have_appeared }
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = -0.9
			capital_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_africa
					geographical_region = world_asia_southeast_islands
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_flag = VIET_genghis_khan_prophecy
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2044.a		
		trigger_event = {
			id = VIETold.2045
		}
	}
}

# Pagan seer prophesizes the decline of polytheism
VIETold.2049 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2049.t
	desc = VIETold.2049.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_callous
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_pagan_future_prophecy }
		faith = {
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_pagan }
			has_doctrine_parameter = unreformed
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		# Less likely in eastern parts of the map where Abrahamic religious wars are less relevant
		modifier = {
			add = -0.7
			capital_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_steppe_tarim
					geographical_region = world_steppe_east
					geographical_region = world_steppe_central
					geographical_region = world_siberia
					geographical_region = world_burma
					geographical_region = world_tibet
					geographical_region = world_asia
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_flag = VIET_pagan_future_prophecy
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2049.a
		trigger_event = {
			id = VIETold.2050
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

# Narri - barmaid flirts with character
VIETold.2054 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2054.t
	desc = VIETold.2054.desc
	theme = friendly	
	override_background = { reference = tavern }
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	trigger = {
		VIET_is_unattractive_trigger = no
		is_female = no
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	option = { # Ignore her
		name = VIETold.2054.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = chaste
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}

	option = { # Chat with her
		name = VIETold.2054.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = chaste
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_interesting_talk_with_stranger
			days = 365
		}
		stress_impact = {
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}

	option = { # Flirt with her
		name = VIETold.2054.c
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_sexuality = homosexual
				has_sexuality = asexual
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_interesting_talk_with_stranger
			days = 365
		}
		stress_impact = {
			chaste = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}

	option = { # Have a one night stand
		name = VIETold.2054.d
		trigger = {
			has_trait = lustful
			NOR = {
				has_sexuality = homosexual
				has_sexuality = asexual
			}
		}
		trait = lustful
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = chaste
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_one_time_lovemaking
			days = 365
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lustful = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}
}

		character = root

	}

		animation = personality_content
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 16 25 }
				gender = female
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = scope_VIET_nice_day_girl
				random_traits_list = {
					count = 1
					education_diplomacy_3 = {}
					education_stewardship_3 = {}
					education_intrigue_3 = {}
				}
				random_traits_list = {
					count = 3
					compassionate = {}
					gregarious = {}
					humble = {}
					generous = {}
					shy = {}
				}
				random_traits = yes
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_nice_day_girl = {
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
				random_list = {
					40 = { }
					40 = { add_trait = beauty_good_1 }
					15 = { add_trait = beauty_good_2 }
					5 = { add_trait = beauty_good_3 }
				}
				#add_character_modifier = {
				#	modifier = VIET_nice_day_girl
				#}
			}			
		}
	}

	option = { # Welcome!
		name = VIETold.2056.a
		add_courtier = scope:scope_VIET_nice_day_girl
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_nice_day_girl
					type = favor_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:scope_VIET_nice_day_girl
				type = favor_hook
			}
		}
	}

		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_jenassa_mercenary_event }
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_serious_events }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_flag = VIET_jenassa_mercenary_event 
	}

	option = { # Hire her
		name = VIETold.2057.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 30
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 30
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_strange_female_bodyguard
			years = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # Don't hire her
		name = VIETold.2057.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}
	option = { # Amusing!
		name = VIETold.2057.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine = doctrine_gender_female_dominated } }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			days = 365
		}
	}
}

# Jon Battle-Born - Getting to know a friendly, poetic guardsman
VIETold.2061 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2061.t
	desc = VIETold.2061.desc
	theme = friendly	
	override_background = { reference = corridor_day }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_compassionate
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_jon_battle_born
		animation = admiration
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 20 35 }
				gender = male
				trait = lifestyle_blademaster
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				diplomacy = { 8 13 }
				martial = { 8 13 }
				prowess = { 4 9 } # Blademaster gives at least 6
				save_scope_as = scope_VIET_jon_battle_born
				random_traits_list = {
					count = 1
					education_diplomacy_3 = {}
					education_martial_3 = {}
				}
				random_traits_list = {
					count = 3
					compassionate = {}
					gregarious = {}
					humble = {}
					generous = {}
					just = {}
					patient = {}
					brave = {}
					calm = {}
				}
				random_traits = yes
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_jon_battle_born = {
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
				random_list = {
					40 = { }
					40 = { add_trait = physique_good_1 }
					15 = { add_trait = physique_good_2 }
					5 = { add_trait = physique_good_3 }
				}
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_jon_battle_born_soldier
				}
				add_random_tiered_trait_xp_effect = {
					TRAIT = lifestyle_blademaster
					LEVEL_1 = yes
					LEVEL_3 = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Welcome!
		name = VIETold.2061.a
		add_courtier = scope:scope_VIET_jon_battle_born
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_jon_battle_born
					type = favor_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:scope_VIET_jon_battle_born
				type = favor_hook
			}
		}
	}
}

# Mithorpa Nasyal (unused NPC) - come across a peasant who initially lashes out but apologises
VIETold.2064 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2064.t
	desc = VIETold.2064.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_tuscan_country
	
	left_portrait = root

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # Forgive him
		name = VIETold.2064.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = forgiving
						trait_is_virtue = calm
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = vengeful
						trait_is_virtue = wrathful
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Get angry
		name = VIETold.2064.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = vengeful
						trait_is_virtue = wrathful
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = forgiving
						trait_is_virtue = calm
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_dread = 5
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Be a dick and lash him
		name = VIETold.2064.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = forgiving
						trait_is_virtue = calm
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_dread = 10
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			calm = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Imprison him
		name = VIETold.2064.d
		trigger = {
			has_trait = wrathful
			NOT = { has_trait = compassionate }
			NOT = { has_trait = humble }
			NOT = { has_trait = forgiving }
		}
		trait = wrathful
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = forgiving
						trait_is_virtue = calm
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_dread = 15
		stress_impact = {
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}


# Sinmir - Elderly townsman criticizes your security

	}

		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	option = { # Ignore him
		name = VIETold.2065.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Ask him what should be done
		name = VIETold.2065.b
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_sinmir_good_defense_advice
					years = 7
				}
			}
			10 = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_sinmir_bad_defense_advice
					years = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Tell him to mind his business
		name = VIETold.2065.c
		add_dread = 5
	}
}

			#}
		}

			#}
		}

		add_character_flag = VIET_skyrim_fake_merchant_suspicion
		trigger_event = VIETold.2067
	}

# Telrav - encounter a robbed "merchant" on the road
VIETold.2067 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2067.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					has_character_flag = VIET_skyrim_fake_merchant_suspicion
				}
				desc = VIETold.2067.desc.b
			}
			desc = VIETold.2067.desc.a
		}
	}
	theme = VIET_theme_skyrim_forest
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_vengeful
	}

	option = { # Retreat!
		name = VIETold.2067.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_skyrim_fake_merchant_suspicion }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 30
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				prowess >= 11
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				prowess <= 5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				martial >= 11
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				martial <= 5
			}
			increase_wounds_effect = {
				REASON = pilgrimage_bandit_attack
			}		
		}
	}
	option = { # We win!
		name = VIETold.2067.b
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = VIET_skyrim_fake_merchant_suspicion
		}
		random = {
			chance = 15
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				prowess >= 11
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				prowess <= 5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				martial >= 11
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				martial <= 5
			}
			increase_wounds_effect = {
				REASON = pilgrimage_bandit_attack
			}		
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_gold = 20 }
			10 = { add_gold = 40 }
			10 = { add_gold = 60 }
			10 = { add_gold = 80 }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_character_flag = VIET_skyrim_fake_merchant_suspicion
	}
}

# Traveling merchant offers to sell you Egyptian sunscreen
VIETold.2072 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2072.t
	desc = VIETold.2072.desc
	theme = love
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		# Should only happen in the Mediterranean, Middle East, and Africa close to Egypt
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_africa_north
				geographical_region = world_africa_east
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_middle_east
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
				geographical_region = world_europe_south
				geographical_region = world_europe_west_iberia
				geographical_region = world_europe_west_francia
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	option = { # Buy the sunscreen
		name = VIETold.2072.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 25
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 30
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_egyptian_sunscreen
			years = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2072.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Haggle with the merchant
		name = VIETold.2072.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 25
			}
			diplomacy >= medium_skill_rating
		}
		skill = diplomacy
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_egyptian_sunscreen
			years = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2072.info
		}
	}
	option = { # No need to buy it
		name = VIETold.2072.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2072.info
		}
	}
}




# Courtier stared at sun for too long
VIETold.2073 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2073.t
	desc = VIETold.2073.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_garden_generic
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = disapproval
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_sun_starer
		animation = grief
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_sun_starer
		}
	}

	option = { # What a dumbass
		name = VIETold.2073.a
		scope:scope_VIET_sun_starer = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_stared_at_sun
						years = 1
					}
				}
				25 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_permanent_sun_damage
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_trait = lifestyle_physician
					has_trait = lifestyle_herbalist
				}
			}
			desc = VIETold.2075.desc.educated
		}
	}
	theme = medicine
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}


	option = { # Buy some herbs
		name = VIETold.2075.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 15
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_purchase_herbs_small
			years = 4
		}
	}
	option = { # Buy a lot of herbs
		name = VIETold.2075.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 45
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 45
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_purchase_herbs_large
			years = 4
		}
	}
	option = { # Just browse for fun
		name = VIETold.2075.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}

# Maid reports your courtier wrote her a creepy love letter and is perving on her
VIETold.2081 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2081.t	
	desc = VIETold.2081.desc
	theme = seduction
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_courtier_perving_on_maid
		animation = personality_dishonorable
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			has_trait = lustful
			is_female = no
			NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
			NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = forgiving
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = vengeful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				has_trait = lustful
				is_female = no
				NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
				NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_courtier_perving_on_maid
		}
	}

	option = { # Ignore the issue
		name = VIETold.2081.a
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_courtier_perving_on_maid = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_loves_cute_maids
				years = 8
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_ignore_maid_harassment
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_maid_harasser
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			chaste = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Tell the guy to stop
		name = VIETold.2081.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_courtier_perving_on_maid = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_loves_cute_maids
				years = 8
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_warned_about_maids
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_maid_harasser
			}			
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_courtier_perving_on_maid
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_rival_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Courtier complains about loud construction noise
VIETold.2086 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2086.t	
	desc = VIETold.2086.desc
	theme = realm
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer
		animation = dismissal
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = impatient
				has_trait = wrathful
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = arbitrary
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = shy
				has_trait = humble
				has_trait = forgiving
			}
			NOT = { is_close_family_of = root }
		}		
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = arbitrary
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = shy
					has_trait = humble
					has_trait = forgiving
				}
				NOT = { is_close_family_of = root }
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer
		}
	}

	option = { # Halt construction
		name = VIETold.2086.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_reduce_construction_noise
			years = 5
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_supported_construction_noise
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Continue with construction, no big deal
		name = VIETold.2086.b
		scope:scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_ignored_construction_noise
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Discuss ways to reduce noise
		name = VIETold.2086.c
		trigger = {
			stewardship >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = stewardship
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_compromise_construction_noise
			}
		}		
	}
	option = { # Convince courtier to put up with it
		name = VIETold.2086.d
		add_diplomacy_lifestyle_xp = minor_lifestyle_xp
		duel = {
			skill = diplomacy
			target = scope:scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer
			10 = { # Failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -1.1
				}
				#modifier = {
				#	factor = 1.2
				#	has_trait = shy
				#}
				#modifier = {
				#	factor = 1.2
				#	has_trait = impatient
				#}
				#modifier = {
				#	factor = 1.2
				#	has_trait = callous
				#}
				desc = VIETold.2086.d.a
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETold.2086.d.toast.failure
					scope:scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_ignored_construction_noise
						}
					}
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 1.1
				}
				#modifier = {
				#	factor = 1.2
				#	has_trait = gregarious
				#}
				#modifier = {
				#	factor = 1.2
				#	has_trait = patient
				#}
				#modifier = {
				#	factor = 1.2
				#	has_trait = compassionate
				#}
				desc = VIETold.2086.d.b
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETold.2086.d.toast.success
					scope:scope_VIET_courtier_noise_complainer = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_compromise_construction_noise
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

# Hearing about the barbarian invasions of Rome

	type = character_event

	desc = VIETold.2088.desc
	theme = learning
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			capital_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_europe
					geographical_region = world_asia_minor
					geographical_region = world_middle_east
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_africa_north
					geographical_region = world_africa_east
					geographical_region = world_steppe_west
					geographical_region = world_steppe_central
				}
			}
			culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
			culture_has_mena_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	option = { # Genseric, father of the Vandals
		name = VIETold.2088.a
		random = {
			chance = 33
			add_diplomacy_skill = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2088.a.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Attila the Hun, Scourge of God

			chance = 33
			add_martial_skill = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2088.b.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Alaric the Goth and Sacker of Rome
		name = VIETold.2088.c
		random = {
			chance = 33
			add_stewardship_skill = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2088.c.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Odoacer, ender of Western Rome
		name = VIETold.2088.d
		random = {
			chance = 33
			add_intrigue_skill = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2088.d.info
		}
	}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2

	}

# Nobleman runs away from criminals trying to kill him
VIETold.2093 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2093.t	
	desc = VIETold.2093.desc
	theme = vassal
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee
		animation = paranoia
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 16 30 }
				gender = male
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee
				random_traits_list = {
					count = 1
					education_diplomacy_2 = {}
					education_martial_2 = {}
					education_stewardship_2 = {}
					education_intrigue_2 = {}
					education_learning_2 = {}
				}
				random_traits = yes
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee = {
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_nobleman_with_criminal_problems
				}
			}		
		}
	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2093.a
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		stress_impact = {
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee
					type = favor_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee
				type = favor_hook
			}
		}
		#hidden_effect = {
		#	scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee = {
		#		death = {
		#			death_reason = death_disappearance
		#		}
		#	}
		#}
	}
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2093.b
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		#hidden_effect = {
		#	scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee = {
		#		death = {
		#			death_reason = death_disappearance
		#		}
		#	}
		#}
	}
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2093.c
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_courtier = scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee			
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee
					type = loyalty_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:scope_VIET_nobleman_refugee
				type = loyalty_hook
			}
		}
	}
}

# Guardsman sees grandparents before dying (common phenomonon at end of life)

	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2104.t	
	desc = VIETold.2104.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = sitting_room }
	
	left_portrait = root

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	option = { # Imagining things
		name = VIETold.2104.a
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = VIETold.2105
			days = { 3 10 }
		}
	}
	option = { # hopefully they meant well
		name = VIETold.2104.b
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = VIETold.2105
			days = { 3 10 }
		}
	}
	option = { # universal mysteries
		name = VIETold.2104.c
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = VIETold.2105
			days = { 3 10 }
		}
	}
}

# Coming across a Myling (Nordic mythology)
VIETold.2110 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2110.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					faith = faith:norse_pagan
				}
				desc = VIETold.2110.desc.religion
			}
			desc = VIETold.2110.desc.culture
		}
	}
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = feast }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_myling_courtier
		animation = personality_content
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		OR = {
			faith = faith:norse_pagan
			culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_north_germanic }
		}
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			OR = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				faith = faith:norse_pagan
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_north_germanic }
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					faith = faith:norse_pagan
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_north_germanic }
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_myling_courtier
		}
	}

	option = { # funny
		name = VIETold.2110.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			days = 1095
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_myling_courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_believe_me_myling
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # it's a lie
		name = VIETold.2110.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_myling_courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_believe_me_myling
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # seemed nice
		name = VIETold.2110.c
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_myling_courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_believes_me_myling
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# The Grim Reaper is an absentminded girl and she stops by after getting lost
VIETold.2113 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2113.t	
	desc = VIETold.2113.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_nightmare
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_cute_death
		animation = admiration
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			location = root.capital_province
			name = "Morana"
			age = { 16 25 }
			gender = female
			faith = root.faith
			culture = root.culture
			dynasty = none
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_cute_death
			trait = education_diplomacy_4
			trait = beauty_good_3
			trait = compassionate
			trait = gregarious
			trait = humble
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_cute_death = {
			VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2113.a
		trigger_event = VIETold.2114
	}
}

# The Grim Reaper is an absentminded girl and she stops by after getting lost - part 3, she was real...?
VIETold.2115 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2115.t	
	desc = VIETold.2115.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_cute_death = {		
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}
			}		
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # That was death?
		name = VIETold.2115.a
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_deaths_blessing
		}
	}	
	option = { # Just a dream
		name = VIETold.2115.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_deaths_blessing
		}
	}
}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = { # Proud
		name = VIETold.2119.a
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # yes - normal
		name = VIETold.2119.b
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}
	option = { # no - normal
		name = VIETold.2119.c
		add_dread = 5

			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # life goes on!

			base = minor_stress_impact_loss
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

# Local townsman accused of having sex with ghosts
VIETold.2125 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2125.t	
	desc = VIETold.2125.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_callous
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}

	option = { # let him go
		name = VIETold.2125.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_let_necrophiliac_go
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # execute him
		name = VIETold.2125.b
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_dread = 10
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_executed_necrophiliac
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			calm = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # imprison him
		name = VIETold.2125.c
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_imprisoned_necrophiliac
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

							is_female = yes

						AND = {
							is_female = no
							has_sexuality = homosexual
						}
					}

			desc = VIETold.2129.desc.female
		}

		animation = personality_content

		}

		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate

# Courtier said something inappropriate
VIETold.2134 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2134.t	
	desc = VIETold.2134.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = shock
	}

	right_portrait = scope:scope_VIET_inappropriate_courtier
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = forgiving
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = vengeful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_inappropriate_courtier
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Chastise
		name = VIETold.2134.a
		scope:scope_VIET_inappropriate_courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_chastised_me_in_public
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_inappropriate_speech
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			patient = minor_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Hinted it was inappropriate
		name = VIETold.2134.b
		VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_inappropriate_courtier = {
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_inappropriate_speech
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Ignored it
		name = VIETold.2134.c
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

		animation = personality_honorable
	}

		VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = no

		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_powerful_chinese_empress_tales }
	}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}

			add = -0.2

		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2

		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = { #will not be as common for realms far from China
			add = -0.5

					geographical_region = world_steppe_central
					geographical_region = world_siberia
					geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				}
			}				
		}
	}

		}
	}

VIETold.2140 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2140.t	
	desc = VIETold.2140.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_africa
				geographical_region = world_steppe_west
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_arabia
				geographical_region = world_steppe_central
				geographical_region = world_siberia
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			faith = {
				religion = { is_in_family = rf_eastern }
			}	
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
	}

	option = { # cool idea
		name = VIETold.2140.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = temperate					
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}		
	}
	option = { # Not the circle of life
		name = VIETold.2140.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes	
	}
	option = { # Only peasants
		name = VIETold.2140.c
		add_dread = 4	
	}
	option = { # We avoid food too
		name = VIETold.2140.d
		trigger = {
			faith = {
				OR = {
					religion = religion:islam_religion
					religion = religion:judaism_religion
					#religion = religion:yazidi_religion
					religion = religion:dualism_religion
				}	
			}
		}
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}
	option = { # Customs are all different
		name = VIETold.2140.e
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
	}
}

		}

		}
	}

		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Indian/Iranian superstition about sneezing

			OR = {

				has_cultural_pillar = heritage_indo_aryan
				has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dravidian
			}
		}		
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
	}

	option = { # silly superstition
		name = VIETold.2158.a
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # drink water just in case
		name = VIETold.2158.b
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = paranoid
			}
			stress_impact = {
				paranoid = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # get water, quickly!
		name = VIETold.2158.c
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = paranoid
			}
			stress_impact = {
				paranoid = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

	}

	}

		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_incest_debate
			years = 3
		}		
	}

	option = { # Ok

		custom_tooltip = VIETold.2161.a.tooltip
	}
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2161.b
		custom_tooltip = VIETold.2161.b.tooltip
	}

		name = VIETold.2161.c
		custom_tooltip = VIETold.2161.c.tooltip
	}
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETold.2161.d
		trigger = {
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		trait = zealous
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		custom_tooltip = VIETold.2161.d.tooltip
	}

# Quack doctor arrested
VIETold.2163 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2163.t	
	desc = VIETold.2163.desc
	theme = corruption
	override_icon = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_medicine.dds"
	}
	
	left_portrait = root

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	option = { # Imprison him
		name = VIETold.2163.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_punished_quack_doctor
			years = 7
		}
	}
	option = { # Make him drink poison
		name = VIETold.2163.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = sadistic
			}	
			stress_impact = {
				sadistic = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {	
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
				forgiving = medium_stress_impact_gain
			}		
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = vengeful
						trait_is_sin = wrathful
						trait_is_sin = sadistic
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = vengeful
						trait_is_virtue = wrathful
						trait_is_virtue = sadistic
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_large_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_dread = 15
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_punished_quack_doctor
			years = 7
		}
	}
	option = { # let him go
		name = VIETold.2163.c
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_dread = 15
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_arbitrary_ruling
			years = 7
		}
	}
}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = greedy

				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = impatient
			}

				has_trait = temperate

				has_trait = calm
			}
		}
	}
