			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = arbitrary
					has_trait = gluttonous
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = impatient
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = temperate
					has_trait = content
					has_trait = calm
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = VIET_broccoli_hater
		}
	}

	option = { # Its okay
		name = VIETold.2172.a
		VIET_random_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:VIET_broccoli_hater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_hate_broccoli
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Don't care
		name = VIETold.2172.b
	}
	option = { # I hate it too
		name = VIETold.2172.c
		VIET_random_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:VIET_broccoli_hater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_also_hates_broccoli
			}
		}
	}
}


# Broccoli vs cauliflower
VIETold.2173 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2173.t	
	desc = VIETold.2173.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	override_background = { reference = corridor_day }
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		capital_province = {
			VIET_is_in_broccoli_region_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
	}

	option = { # broccoli
		name = VIETold.2173.a
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_healthy_vegetables
			years = 2
		}
	}
	option = { # cauliflower
		name = VIETold.2173.b
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_healthy_vegetables
			years = 2
		}
	}
	option = { # Am fine with either
		name = VIETold.2173.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_healthy_vegetables
			years = 2
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}
	option = { # Why not both
		name = VIETold.2173.d
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_healthy_vegetables
			years = 2
		}
	}
}

		animation = happiness
	}

			is_available_ai_adult = yes

				target = root
				value > 0
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes

					target = root
					value > 0
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = cafe_friend
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2175.a
		trigger_event = VIETold.2176
	}
}

# Dream of a Korean Drama (probably should've been considered an event chain but oh well)
VIETold.2177 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2177.t	
	desc = VIETold.2177.desc
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = study }

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_generic_kdrama_happened_to_me }
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_serious_events }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_character_flag = VIET_generic_kdrama_happened_to_me
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_girls_pov }
				1 = { add_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_boys_pov }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Who am I?
		name = VIETold.2177.a
		trigger_event = VIETold.2178
	}
}

					has_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_girls_pov

				desc = VIETold.2178.desc.female_lead # Enter the plucky determined naive generic female lead
			}
			desc = VIETold.2178.desc.male_lead # Enter the hot brooding jerk with a heart of gold who takes hot brooding showers
		}
	}
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = study }

	option = { # talk
		name = VIETold.2178.a
		trigger_event = VIETold.2179
	}
}

# Wake up
VIETold.2181 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2181.t	
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					has_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_girls_pov
				}
				desc = VIETold.2181.desc.female_lead
			}
			desc = VIETold.2181.desc.male_lead
		}
	}
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = bedchamber }

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2181.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			chaste = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_girls_pov
			}
			remove_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_girls_pov
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_kdrama_dream_girls_pov
				years = 8
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_boys_pov
			}
			remove_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_boys_pov
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_kdrama_dream_boys_pov
				years = 8
			}
		}
	}
}

# Meeting the Dreamer while lost in a dream - part of VIET lore about the Dreamers
VIETold.2185 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2185.t	
	desc = VIETold.2185.desc
	theme = VIET_scarborough_fair
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:dreamer
		animation = personality_content
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.8
			has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		# Choose whether to meet the male or female Dreamer
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male } }
					set_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					change_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
						add = 1
					}		
				}
				character:VIET_character_001 = {
					save_scope_as = dreamer
				}
			}
			10 = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female } }
					set_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					change_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
						add = 1
					}		
				}
				character:VIET_character_002 = {
					save_scope_as = dreamer
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2185.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer }
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2185.b
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = VIETold.2186
	}

}

# Meeting the Dreamer while lost in a dream - part of VIET lore about the Dreamers
VIETold.2186 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2186.t	
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer
				}
				desc = VIETold.2186.desc.dreamer
			}
			desc = VIETold.2186.desc.not_dreamer
		}
	}
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = bedchamber }

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2186.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:dreamer = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_vague_dream_of_dreamer_female
				years = 10
			}
		}
		else = {			
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_vague_dream_of_dreamer_male
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2186.b
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:dreamer = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_vague_dream_of_dreamer_female
				years = 10
			}
		}
		else = {			
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_vague_dream_of_dreamer_male
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

}

	# 	character = root
	# 	animation = happiness
	# }

	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_campfire_dream
			years = 4
		}
	}

	option = { # Reality
		name = VIETold.2188.a
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}

	option = { # Dream
		name = VIETold.2188.b
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}

	option = { # Cannot distinguish between the two
		name = VIETold.2188.c
		random_list = {
			75 = { VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes }
			25 = { VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { # Dream within a dream
		name = VIETold.2188.d
		random_list = {
			75 = { VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			25 = { VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
	}
}




#############################################
# Spices and Herbs (A-L mostly) 2189-2210
#############################################

# In eastern religions, garlic and onion makes you horny - cut down on it?
VIETold.2189 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2189.t	
	desc = VIETold.2189.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = bp1_kitchen_western }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = boredom
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:chaplain
		animation = disapproval
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			religion = religion:buddhism_religion
			religion = religion:taoism_religion
			religion = religion:hinduism_religion
			religion = religion:jainism_religion
		}
		exists = cp:councillor_court_chaplain
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			is_available_healthy_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			save_scope_as = chaplain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2189.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_trait = lustful }
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		scope:chaplain = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -10
				target = root
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			chaste = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2189.info
		}
	}

	option = { # eat less
		name = VIETold.2189.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_reducing_garlic_onion
			years = 10
		}
		scope:chaplain = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 10
				target = root
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			gluttonous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2189.info
		}
	}

	option = { # I want to be horny
		name = VIETold.2189.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		trait = lustful
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		scope:chaplain = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -10
				target = root
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			chaste = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2189.info
		}
	}


	option = { # eat none
		name = VIETold.2189.d
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_avoiding_garlic_onion
			years = 10
		}
		scope:chaplain = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 20
				target = root
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			gluttonous = major_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2189.info
		}
	}

}

# Courtier comes to a mosque after eating garlic
VIETold.2190 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2190.t	
	desc = VIETold.2190.desc
	theme = faith
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = disgust
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:garlic_eater
		animation = shame
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		religion = religion:islam_religion
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			faith = root.faith
			OR = {
				has_trait = gluttonous
				has_trait = cynical
				has_trait = lazy
				has_trait = impatient
				has_trait = trusting
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = stubborn
			}
			NOT = { has_trait = zealous }
			NOT = { has_trait = temperate }
		}

	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				faith = root.faith
				OR = {
					has_trait = gluttonous
					has_trait = cynical
					has_trait = lazy
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = trusting
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = stubborn
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = zealous }
				NOT = { has_trait = temperate }
			}
			save_scope_as = garlic_eater
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_ate_garlic_mosque
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2190.a
		stress_impact = {
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2190.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:garlic_eater = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_corrected_error
				target = root
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # kick them out
		name = VIETold.2190.c
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = minor_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:garlic_eater = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_kicked_out_of_mosque
				target = root
			}
		}
	}

}



# Debating about where cinnamon comes from
VIETold.2191 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2191.t	
	desc = VIETold.2191.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_kitchen_generic
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	lower_left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier_1
		trigger = { exists = scope:courtier_1 }
	}
	lower_center_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier_2
		trigger = { exists = scope:courtier_2 }
	}
	lower_right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier_3
		trigger = { exists = scope:courtier_3 }
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			count >= 3
		}
		NOT = { religion = religion:islam_religion }
		NOT = { religion = religion:zoroastrianism_religion }
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_africa_north
				geographical_region = world_africa_sahara
				geographical_region = world_africa_west
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_steppe
				geographical_region = world_asia_north_east
				geographical_region = world_asia_korea
				geographical_region = world_asia_japan
				geographical_region = world_asia_sakhalin_hokkaido
				geographical_region = world_siberia
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = cinnamon_chat_candidates
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = cinnamon_chat_candidates
			save_scope_as = courtier_1
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = cinnamon_chat_candidates
			limit = {
				exists = scope:courtier_1
				NOT = { this = scope:courtier_1 }
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier_2
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = cinnamon_chat_candidates
			limit = {
				exists = scope:courtier_1
				exists = scope:courtier_2
				NOT = { this = scope:courtier_1 }
				NOT = { this = scope:courtier_2 }
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier_3
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2191.a
		scope:courtier_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_cinnamon_agree
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2191.info
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2191.b
		scope:courtier_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_cinnamon_agree
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2191.info
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2191.c
		scope:courtier_3 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_cinnamon_agree
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETold.2191.info
		}
	}
	
}

	}

		OR = {
			culture = {
				OR = {

				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_india

					geographical_region = world_burma
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_arabia
					geographical_region = world_africa_east
					geographical_region = world_steppe_tarim
				}
			}

		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2192.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_dhana_jiru
			years = 3
		}
	}
	
}

# Bathe in saffron as an aphrodasiac?
VIETold.2194 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2194.t	
	desc = VIETold.2194.desc
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = relaxing_room }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = flirtation
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			culture = {
				OR = {
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_indo_aryan
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dravidian
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tocharian
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_burman
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iberian
				}
			}
			capital_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_india
					geographical_region = world_steppe_tarim
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_middle_east
					geographical_region = world_africa_north
					geographical_region = world_asia_minor
					geographical_region = world_europe_south_east
					geographical_region = world_europe_west_iberia
				}
			}

		}
		VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2194.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 20
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_saffron_aphrodisiac
			years = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = chaste
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = lustful
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			chaste = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2194.b
		stress_impact = {
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
}


# Wood avens growing at home
VIETold.2195 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2195.t	
	desc = {
		desc = VIETold.2195.desc
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					religion = religion:christianity_religion
				}
				desc = VIETold.2195.desc.christian
			}
		}
	}
	theme = VIET_theme_garden_generic
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = admiration
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
				geographical_region = world_steppe_west
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2195.a
		remove_short_term_gold = 5
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_wood_avens
			years = 5
		}
		#VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2195.b
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
}

# Snack of quark cheese and chives
VIETold.2197 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2197.t	
	desc = VIETold.2197.desc

# Visiting someone hanging chives from their doorways
VIETold.2198 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2198.t	
	desc = VIETold.2198.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_kitchen_generic
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:vassal
		animation = personality_content
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_steppe
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_siberia
				geographical_region = world_asia_korea
				geographical_region = world_asia_japan
			}
		}
		any_vassal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
			capital_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_europe
					geographical_region = world_steppe
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
					geographical_region = world_asia_minor
					geographical_region = world_siberia
					geographical_region = world_asia_korea
					geographical_region = world_asia_japan
				}
			}			
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
				capital_province = {
					OR = {
						geographical_region = world_europe
						geographical_region = world_steppe
						geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
						geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
						geographical_region = world_asia_minor
						geographical_region = world_siberia
						geographical_region = world_asia_korea
						geographical_region = world_asia_japan
					}
				}			
			}
			save_scope_as = vassal
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_chives_everywhere
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2198.a
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2198.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 25
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_chives_everywhere
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2198.c
		VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
}

# Clove oil to help with headaches
VIETold.2200 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2200.t	
	desc = VIETold.2200.desc
	theme = physical_health
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = stress
	}
	right_portrait = scope:physician

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		court_physician_available_trigger = yes
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_court_physician_as_effect = { SCOPE_NAME = physician }
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_mild_headaches
			years = 7
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2200.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 30
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 30
		remove_character_modifier = VIET_mild_headaches
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2200.b
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
}

# Courtier thinks the grains of paradise actually came from heaven
VIETold.2203 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2203.t	
	desc = VIETold.2203.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = laugh
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:grains_of_paradise_dumb
		animation = shame
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_steppe_west
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				probably_unintelligent_trigger = yes
				has_trait = trusting
				learning <= low_skill_rating
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					probably_unintelligent_trigger = yes
					has_trait = trusting
					learning <= low_skill_rating
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = grains_of_paradise_dumb
			VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		}
		# every_courtier_or_guest = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		NOT = { this = scope:grains_of_paradise_dumb }
		# 	}
		# 	custom = all_courtiers_and_guests			
		# 	reverse_add_opinion = {
		# 		target = scope:grains_of_paradise_dumb
		# 		modifier = humiliated_opinion
		# 		opinion = -5
		# 	}
		# }
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2203.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			days = 365
		}		
		scope:grains_of_paradise_dumb = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = humiliated_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2203.b	
		scope:grains_of_paradise_dumb = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = grateful_opinion
				opinion = 5
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2203.c
		trigger = {
			learning >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = learning
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_impressed_others_with_knowledge
			days = 365
		}
	}
	
}

	}

		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_annoying_insects
			years = 10
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2209.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 30
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 30
		remove_character_modifier = VIET_annoying_insects
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_effective_pest_control
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2209.b
		stress_impact = {
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
}

		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {

		}
	}

	immediate = {

				tier = tier_county					
				is_landless_type_title = no
			}
			save_scope_as = county
		}
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_generic_middle_aged_male_template
			save_scope_as = edgar
		}
	}

	option = { # ok

				is_ai = no
				gold >= 15
			}

		}

			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2216.b
	}

	after = {			
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:edgar = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}

}

# Ontus Vanin - scholar who's retired, stays behind and reads trashy books
VIETold.2220 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2220.t	
	desc = VIETold.2220.desc
	theme = learning
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:ontus_vanin
		animation = personality_content
	}



	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
	}

	immediate = {	
		random_sub_realm_county = {
			limit = {
				tier = tier_county					
				is_landless_type_title = no
			}
			save_scope_as = county
		}
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_ontus_vanin_template
			save_scope_as = ontus_vanin
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2220.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}		
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:ontus_vanin = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2220.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}		
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:ontus_vanin = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2220.c		
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		duel = {
			skill = diplomacy
			target = scope:ontus_vanin
			15 = { # Failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -1.1
				}
				desc = VIETold.2220.c.toast.failure
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:ontus_vanin
					title = VIETold.2220.c.toast.failure		
					hidden_effect = {
						scope:ontus_vanin = {
							death = {
								death_reason = death_vanished
							}
						}			
					}
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 1.1
				}
				desc = VIETold.2220.c.toast.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = scope:ontus_vanin
					title = VIETold.2220.c.toast.success
					add_courtier = scope:ontus_vanin					
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

# Meet a crazy madwoman - Runs-In-Circles
# VIET_nick_runs_in_circles
VIETold.2222 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2222.t	
	desc = VIETold.2222.desc
	theme = mental_health
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = schadenfreude
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:runs_in_circles
		animation = paranoia
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_all_events
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {	
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_runs_in_circles_template
			save_scope_as = runs_in_circles
		}
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_generic_middle_aged_male_template
			save_scope_as = runs_in_circles_husband			
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:runs_in_circles = {
				give_nickname = VIET_nick_runs_in_circles
				marry = scope:runs_in_circles_husband
			}
			scope:runs_in_circles_husband = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_natural_causes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2222.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:runs_in_circles = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2222.b
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:runs_in_circles = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2222.c
		VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_courtier = scope:runs_in_circles
	}

}

# The pasta you're eating is bland
VIETold.2234 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2234.t	
	desc = VIETold.2234.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = dismissal
	}

	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin }
			capital_province = {
				geographical_region = world_europe_south_italy
			}			
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2234.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2234.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = arbitrary
					has_trait = vengeful
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				wrathful = medium_stress_impact_loss
				arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_loss
				sadistic = minor_stress_impact_loss
				vengeful = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
				patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				content = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_heartless_towards_servants
			years = 5
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETold.2234.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = arbitrary
					has_trait = vengeful
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				wrathful = minor_stress_impact_loss
				arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				content = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		add_dread = 5
	}

}

# Vassal does not want to wash hands with rosewater at a feast
VIETold.2235 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2235.t	
	desc = VIETold.2235.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:vassal
		animation = personality_callous
	}

	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		any_vassal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOR = {
				has_trait = diligent
				has_trait = scholar
				has_trait = craven
				has_trait = humble
				has_trait = patient
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
	}


	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = diligent
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = humble
					has_trait = patient
				}		
			}
			save_scope_as = vassal
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_doesnt_do_rosewater_handwashing
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Don't care
		name = VIETold.2235.a
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # Chastise them
		name = VIETold.2235.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_chastised_me_in_public
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Copy them
		name = VIETold.2235.c
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_doesnt_do_rosewater_handwashing
			years = 10
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 10
				target = root
			}
		}
	}

}

# Come across a black cat
VIETold.2236 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2236.t	
	desc = VIETold.2236.desc
	theme = mental_break
	override_background = { reference = courtyard }
	
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = fear
	}

	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		# Won't happen for cultures and faiths where black cats are seen as good, revered, or have a more mixed reputation
		NOR = {
			culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_chinese }
			culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_goidelic }
			culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_brythonic }
			culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic }
			religion = religion:islam_religion
			religion = religion:kushitism_religion			
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = eccentric
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
	}

	option = { # Ahhh
		name = VIETold.2236.a
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
			brave = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # Who cares
		name = VIETold.2236.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		random = {
			chance = 40
			send_interface_toast = {
				type = event_toast_effect_bad
				left_icon = ROOT
				title = VIETold.2236.b.toast.failure
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_black_cat_bad_luck
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = brave
			}
			stress_impact = {
				brave = minor_stress_impact_loss
				arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_gain
				craven = minor_stress_impact_gain
				paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
	}

}

				}

					years = 9
				}
			}
			10 = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_mild_insomnia
					years = 10
				}
			}
			10 = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_mild_insomnia
					years = 11
				}
			}
			10 = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_mild_insomnia
					years = 12
				}

			add = 0.2

		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2

		}

			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}


	option = { # ok

# Traveler helps guards take down gang of female thieves who use seduction (Oblivion/Anvil reference)
VIETold.2245 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2245.t	
	desc = {
		desc = VIETold.2245.desc
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					scope:adventurer = {
						is_female = yes
					}
				}
				desc = VIETold.2245.desc.female
			}
			desc = VIETold.2245.desc.male
		}
		desc = VIETold.2245.desc.end
	}
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	# left_portrait = {
	# 	character = root
	# 	animation = throne_room_applaud_1

		}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {	
		random_held_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = tier_county					
				is_landless_type_title = no
			}
			save_scope_as = county
		}
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_siren_gang_defeater_traveler_template
			faith = scope:county.faith
			culture = scope:county.culture

	option = { # No reward
		name = VIETold.2245.a

			random = {
				chance = 80
				scope:adventurer = {
					death = {
						death_reason = death_vanished
					}
				}
			}			
		}
		
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # Standard reward
		name = VIETold.2245.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 30
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 30
		VIET_massive_prestige_gain_effect = yes

					death = {

					}
				}
			}			
		}
		
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # Invite them to the court
		name = VIETold.2245.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 50
			}
		}

			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}


}

# Stories about a tropical paradise
VIETold.2248 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2248.t	
	desc = VIETold.2248.desc
	theme = realm
	override_background = { reference = docks }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = throne_room_conversation_3
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}

	trigger = {
		any_held_county = {
			is_landless_type_title = no
			is_coastal_county = yes	
		}
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
		scope:courtier = {			
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_thinking_about_foreign_lands
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Doubt
		name = VIETold.2248.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_skeptical_ruler
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # Believe in it
		name = VIETold.2248.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_thinking_about_foreign_lands
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	option = { # What faith?
		name = VIETold.2248.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_religion_in_faraway_lands
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}


}

# Song of Scarborough Fair
VIETold.2249 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2249.t	
	desc = VIETold.2249.desc
	theme = diplomacy
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = admiration
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:adventurer
		animation = personality_content
	}


	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
	}


	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {	
		random_held_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = tier_county					
				is_landless_type_title = no
			}
			save_scope_as = county
		}
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_generic_elder_local_template
			faith = scope:county.faith
			culture = scope:county.culture
			save_scope_as = adventurer
		}
	}

	option = { # Doubt
		name = VIETold.2249.a
		trigger_event = VIETold.2250
	}


}

# Lesson of Scarborough Fair
VIETold.2250 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETold.2250.t	
	desc = VIETold.2250.desc
	theme = diplomacy
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = admiration
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:adventurer
		animation = lute_active
	}



	option = {
		name = VIETold.2250.a
		custom_tooltip = VIETold.2250.a.tooltip
		add_piety = 888
		add_prestige = 888
		dynasty ?= {
			add_dynasty_prestige = 888
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_scarborough_fair_lesson
		}
	}

	after = {			
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:adventurer = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}

}
